VISUALIZATION SUMMARY
================================================================================

 STANDARD VISUALIZATIONS (5 charts):
  1. ✓ Gantt Chart              - Train schedules over time
  2. ✓ Synchronization Network  - Train-flight connections by station
  3. ✓ Demand Coverage Analysis - 4-panel demand dashboard
  4. ✓ Quality Metrics          - 6-panel performance dashboard
  5. ✓ Time-Space Diagram       - Train trajectories

 DEMAND VISUALIZATIONS (4 charts):
  6. ✓ Demand Heatmap          - Coverage by station and time
  7. ✓ Flight Ranking          - Flights ranked by demand
  8. ✓ Train Productivity      - Passengers served per train
  9. ✓ Connection Quality      - Transfer time vs penalty

 FILES SAVED TO: './visualizations/'
  • gantt_chart.html
  • synchronization_network.html
  • demand_coverage.html
  • quality_metrics.html
  • time_space_diagram.html
  • demand_heatmap.html
  • flight_ranking.html
  • train_productivity.html
  • connection_quality.html

 KEY INSIGHTS:
  • Passenger Coverage: 35.7% (4,188/11,747 passengers)
  • Flight Coverage: 26/81 flights (32.1%)
  • Total Synchronizations: 29
  • Average connections per covered flight: 1.1
  • Best performing station: Station 2 (37.8% coverage)
  • Most productive train: Train 7 (627 passengers)
